<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rok.html>rok</a> (6000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roc.html>roc</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:rok.html>rok</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rukkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>skirt <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">clothing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>full dress, white tie <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">formal clothing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***roken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a> (1528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rôken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke (a tobacco product, another drug, a surrogate)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sigaret.html>sigaret</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b>are smoking</b> a cigarette.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">But I <b>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> smoke</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>Vroeger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> in zeemansbuurten <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> opium <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerookt.html>gerookt</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">People used to <b>smoke</b> a lot of opium in the sailors' <a href = vnd.unilang:districts.html>districts</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke, to produce smoke
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rookte.html>rookte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:enorm.html>enorm</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The engine <b>produced</b> a great amount of <b>smoke</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> plural past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiken.html>ruiken</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention"> plural past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rieken.html>rieken</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgeven.html>afgeven</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rookt.html>rookt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweldig.html>geweldig</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rollenspel.html>rollenspel</a> (26050)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a></i>, likely a calque.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollenspel.html>rollenspel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollenspelen.html>rollenspelen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollenspellen.html>rollenspellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollenspel.html>rollenspelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A role playing game. <span class="defdate">[early or mid 20th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rollen.html>rollen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***rome.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>rome</a> (1536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*Rōma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Rūmō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">rōme</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a></span> (a city in modern <span class="Latn" lang="en">Italy</span>)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***ronin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ronin.html>ronin</a> (63195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">浪人</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">ろうにん, rōnin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Chinese">Middle Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc">浪</i> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> "wave", by extension "adrift") + <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc">人</i> (<i>nyin</i> "person").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ronin.html>ronin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ronins</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ronin.html>ronin</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A masterless samurai (who often becomes a mercenary to make <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> meet).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in Japan</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A student who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> failed the entrance examination for the high school or university of their choice: if the student does not wish to take the exam the following year or <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unable to, the student becomes a <a href = vnd.unilang:ronin.html>ronin</a>, assuming full responsibility for their own training and survival.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rôot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raudaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rowdʰós</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rewdʰ-</i>.
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> left, socialist, labor</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roof</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roven.html>roven</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>predator</li>
<li>carnivore
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vleeseter.html>vleeseter</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carnivoor.html>carnivoor</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>carnivoran, any member of the order Carnivora</li></ol>
